757	def test_firefox_version_supports_released_edge_cases(version_string):
758	    assert str(FirefoxVersion.parse(version_string)) == version_string
759	    for klass in (DeveditionVersion, FennecVersion, ThunderbirdVersion):
760	        if klass == FennecVersion and version_string in (
761	            "33.1",
762	            "33.1build1",
763	            "33.1build2",
764	        ):
765	            # These edge cases also exist in Fennec
766	            continue
767	        with pytest.raises(PatternNotMatchedError):
768	            klass.parse(version_string)

746	        "33.1build2",
747	        "33.1build3",

753	        "38.0.5b3",
754	        "38.0.5b3build1",
755	    ),
756	)
757	def test_firefox_version_supports_released_edge_cases(version_string):
758	    assert str(FirefoxVersion.parse(version_string)) == version_string
759	    for klass in (DeveditionVersion, FennecVersion, ThunderbirdVersion):
760	        if klass == FennecVersion and version_string in (
761	            "33.1",
762	            "33.1build1",
763	            "33.1build2",
764	        ):
765	            # These edge cases also exist in Fennec
766	            continue
767	        with pytest.raises(PatternNotMatchedError):
768	            klass.parse(version_string)
